             <div class="search-inner">
              <input autocapitalize="off" autocomplete="off" autocorrect="off" class="form-control" data-sv-searchinput="" name="q" placeholder="Search..." type="text"/>

          <script>
           require(['jquery'], function($) {
		var root = $('[data-guid="df895197-ca47-4b23-aaed-380fda97a75c"]');
		var mobile = root.find('[data-sv-search-mobile]');

		root.find('[data-sv-searchBtn]').on('click', function() {
			$(this).closest('[data-sv-searchForm]').submit();
		});

		root.find('[data-sv-searchForm]').submit(function(e) {
			if ($(this).find('[data-sv-searchInput]').val().length === 0) {
				e.preventDefault();
			}
		});

		$('[data-sv-search-mobile-container]').replaceWith(mobile);
		mobile.removeClass('hide');

		init_search_popup();

		/*----------  Init Search Popup  ----------*/

		function init_search_popup() {
			var $header = $('header').first();
			var $search_popup = $('#search_popup');

			if ($search_popup.length) {
				var $btn = $('.btn_search_popup');
				var $txt_search = $search_popup.find('.txt_search');

				$btn.off('click').on('click', function() {
					var $this = $(this);

					if (!$search_popup.is(':visible')) {
						if ($(this).hasClass('animate')) {
							$('body').animate({
								scrollTop: $('header').offset().top
							}, 1000, function() {
								open_popup();
							});
						} else {
							open_popup();
						}
					} else {
						close_popup();
					}

					return false;
				});

				$txt_search.off('blur').on('blur', function() {
					var val = $.trim($(this).val());

					if (val == null || val == "") {
						close_popup();
					}
				});

				var open_popup = function() {
					var header_height = $header.innerHeight();
					var header_top = parseInt($header.offset().top + header_height);

					$btn.addClass('open');
					$('body').css('overflow', 'hidden');
					// .css('top', header_top + 'px')
					$search_popup.fadeIn('fast', function() {
						$txt_search.focus();
					});
				}

				var close_popup = function() {
					$btn.removeClass('open');
					$search_popup.fadeOut('fast');
					$('body').css('overflow', '');
				}
			}
		}
	});
          </script>

                 <script>
                  require(['jquery','domReady!'], function($) {
		var root = $('[data-guid="07b89067-07e4-414e-a84f-c7e128ea38e4"]');
		var mobile = root.find('[data-sv-nav-main-mobile]');
		var navItemProperties = JSON.parse($('meta[name=sv-nav-properties]').attr('content'));
		var parents_ids = navItemProperties.parents_ids || [];
		var currentSectionId = parents_ids.length ? parents_ids[0] : navItemProperties.id;

		/* t331707 - This is to get the parent folder and see if it's 'partners'*/

		var url = $(location).prop("pathname");
		var parts = url.split("/");
		var parent = parts[1];

		if(parent === "partners") {
			var partnerRoot = root.find('.partners');
			partnerRoot.addClass('open');
			root.find('.partners > ul').css('display', 'block');
		}

		/**********/

		parents_ids.forEach(function(id) {
			mobile.find('[data-id="' + id + '"]')
				.addClass('open selected')
				.children('ul')
				.addClass('open');
		});

		root.find('[data-id="' + navItemProperties.id + '"]')
			.addClass('selected')
			.prop('selected', true);

		$('[data-sv-nav-main-mobile-container]').replaceWith(mobile);
		mobile.removeClass('hide');
	});
                 </script>

               <div class="contentRender contentRender_4 contentRender_type_widget contentRender_name_plugins_tripbuilder_counter" data-gtm-vars='{ "tCore" : { "contentNum" : "1" } }' data-sv-index="4" data-sv-time="15">

                <script>
                 require(["jquery", "site_tripbuilder"], function($, tripbuilder) {
		if (!tripbuilder.enabled) { return; }

		var root = $("#tripbuilder_counter_73980992-159c-477d-9eca-1296a5b9bcf3");
		var container = $("[data-sv-tripbuilderCounter]");
		var renderContainer = root.closest(".contentRender_name_plugins_tripbuilder_tripbuilder_counter");
		container.append(renderContainer);
		var onChangeCB = function() {
			root.html("<a href='" + tripbuilder.path + "'><span class='atn-inner'><span class='atn-badge bg-theme'>" + tripbuilder.getTotalCount() + "</span><span class='atn-icon'><span class='fa fa-suitcase'></span></span></span></a>");

			$('[data-sv-tripbuilder-container]').replaceWith("<a href='" + tripbuilder.path + "'><span class='atn-inner'><span class='atn-badge'>" + tripbuilder.getTotalCount() + "</span><span class='atn-icon'><span class='fa fa-suitcase'></span></span></span></a>");
		}
		onChangeCB();
		tripbuilder.events.on("change", onChangeCB);
	});
                </script>

          require(["jquery"], function() {
		// This should exist in the header panel and adds the body class as quickly as possible to hide
		// all the items on the page so we don't have the site flash before the calendar shows up
		if (location.search.indexOf('action=popupCal') > -1 && document.body.querySelectorAll('.lookup-calHolder')) {
			document.body.classList.add('crm-calendar-popup');
		};
	})

              <div class="global-slick-controls slick-controls" id="jumbotron_slick_controls">
               <div class="slick-nav slick_nav">

            <script>
             require(['jquery', 'lodash', 'sv_siteSlick', 'plugins_common_custom_magnific'], function($, lodash) {
		var root = $('[data-guid="affba577-4667-444b-9d2c-bac0efb50f48"]');

		init_jumbotron_slick();

		setSrc(root.find('.item[data-sv-index="1"] .item-media'));
		loadVideo(root.find('.item[data-sv-index="1"] video'));

		root.find('[data-sv-play]').magnificPopup({
			type: 'iframe',
			mainClass: 'mfp-fade',
			removalDelay: 160,
			preloader: false,
			fixedContentPos: false
		});

		var listenScroll = function() {
			var videoHeight = root.find('.slide.slick-active').height();
			var windowScrollPosition = $(this).scrollTop();

			if (windowScrollPosition > videoHeight) {
				root.find('.slide.slick-active video').each(function() {
					this.pause();
					$(this).removeClass('playing');
				});
			} else {
				root.find('.slide.slick-active video').each(function() {
					this.play();
					$(this).addClass('playing');
				});
			}

			root.find('#jumbotron_slick').slick('setPosition')
		}

		$(window).on('resize', lodash.debounce(listenScroll, 500));

		var $yt_player_actions = root.find('#yt_player_actions');
		var $atn_playback = $yt_player_actions.find('.atn_playback');
		var $atn_sound = $yt_player_actions.find('.atn_sound');

		$atn_playback.off('click').on('click', function() {
			if ($(this).hasClass('active')) {
				$(this).closest('.item').find('video').each(function() {
					this.play();
					$(this).addClass('playing');
				});
				$(this).removeClass('active');
			} else {
				$(this).closest('.item').find('video').each(function() {
					this.pause();
					$(this).removeClass('playing');
				});
				$(this).addClass('active');
			}
		});

		$atn_sound.off('click').on('click', function() {
			if ($(this).hasClass('active')) {
				$(this).closest('.item').find('video').each(function() {
					$(this).prop('muted', true);
				});
				$(this).removeClass('active');
			} else {
				$(this).closest('.item').find('video').each(function() {
					$(this).prop('muted', false);
				});
				$(this).addClass('active');
			}
		});

		function loadVideo(node) {
			node.each(function() {
				var video = this;

				if (!$(video).hasClass('loaded')) {
					$(video).attr('src', $(video).attr('data-src'));
					video.load();
					$(video).on('loadeddata', function() {
						this.play();
						$(video).addClass('loaded playing');
					});
				} else {
					video.play();
					$(video).addClass('playing');
				}
			});
		}

		function setSrc(node) {
			node.each(function() {
				if (!$(this).hasClass('loaded')) {
					$(this).css({ 'background-image' : 'url("' + $(this).attr('data-bgi') + '")' });
					$(this).addClass('loaded');
				}
			});
		}

		function init_jumbotron_slick() {
			var $slick = root.find('#jumbotron_slick');
			var $slick_controls = root.find('#jumbotron_slick_controls');
			var $slick_nav = $slick_controls.find('.slick_nav');
			var $slick_paging = $slick_controls.find('.slick_paging');

			$slick.on("beforeChange", function(event, slick, current, next) {
				root.find('video.playing').each(function() {
					this.pause();
					$(this).removeClass('playing');
				});

				setSrc(root.find(".item[data-slick-index=" + next + "] .item-media"));
				loadVideo(root.find(".item[data-slick-index=" + next + "] video"));
			});

			$slick.slick({
				speed: 700,
				fade: true,
				dots: true,
				arrows: true,
				infinite: true,
				slidesToShow: 1,
				slidesToScroll: 1,
				autoplaySpeed: 2000,
				adaptiveHeight: true,
				appendDots: $slick_paging,
				appendArrows: $slick_nav,
				prevArrow: '<span class="slick-arrow slick-prev slick_prev"><span class="fa fa-angle-left"></span></span>',
				nextArrow: '<span class="slick-arrow slick-next slick_next"><span class="fa fa-angle-right"></span></span>',
				customPaging: function(e, i) {
					var slide_index = i + 1;

					return "<span>" + slide_index + "</span>";
				}
			});
		}

		root.closest('body').addClass('homepage');
	});
            </script>
           </div>
          </div>
         </section>
         <script>
          require(['jquery'], function($) {
		setTimeout(function() {
			$('#cnt_mega_jumbotron').addClass('nav-open');
		}, 200);
	});
         </script>
        </div>

                           </a>
                          </h3>

                         <div class="block-description">
                          <p>
                           North Carolinas capital is a hot-spot destination for foodies and culture seekers alike, with restaurants founded by nationally-acclaimed chefs, an abundance of arts offerings, happening music venues, a world-class set of museums and more. And it certainly helps that the City of Oaks has been recognized as one of "America's Favorite Food Cities" by Travel and Leisure, called one of the "Hottest Food Cities of the Year" by Zagat and racked up a whole bunch of James Beard Foundation Award nominations in recent years. With 48 hours in Raleigh, you can hit some of the most noted places to eat and drinkweve curated a two-day itinerary packed with a plethora of things to do!

          <div class="contentRender contentRender_14 contentRender_type_widget contentRender_name_plugins_social_stackla_template_slider" data-gtm-vars='{ "tCore" : { "contentNum" : "1" } }' data-sv-index="14" data-sv-time="16">

            <script data-sv-template="" type="text/template">
             {{:data}}
				{{#data}}
					<div class="slide">

           <script>
            require([
		"jquery",
		"sv_goatee!plugins=stringLib,cloudinary",
		"sv_asyncLib",
		"sv_siteSlick",
		"plugins_common_custom_magnific"
	], function(
		$,
		goatee,
		asyncLib,
		magnific
	) {
		var root = $("#stackla_4cd08133-8542-4dfe-955c-4f9d7d8c1ade");
		var slider = root.find(".slides");
		var filterId = 72944;
		var stackId = 1970
		var template = root.find("[data-sv-template]").html();

		var flow = new asyncLib.Flow();
		flow.series({
			data : function(cb) {
				$.get("/includes/plugins/social/stackla/", { endpoint : "filterById", stackId : stackId, args : { filterId : filterId, limit : 10, include_pinned : 1 } }).done(function(res) {
					cb(null, res.data);
				}).fail(function(err, type, message) {
					return cb(new Error(message));
				});
			},
			render : function(cb) {
				//perform any alterations needed to data before render
				console.log("sd", flow.data.data);
				flow.data.data.forEach(function(val) {
					if (val.source === "twitter") {
						// append @ for twitter users
						val.user = "@" + val.user;
					} else if (val.source === "facebook" || val.source === "instagram") {
						if(val.name == ""){
							val.name = val.user;
						}
						// user is the same value as name, resulting in repetition
						delete val.user;
					}

					val.filterId = filterId;
				});

				var html = goatee.fill(template, { data : flow.data.data });

				root.find("[data-sv-items]").html(html);

				slider.on("init", function() {
					root.css({ visibility : "visible" });
				});

				slider.slick({
					prevArrow : root.find(".prevSlide"),
					nextArrow : root.find(".nextSlide"),
					slidesToShow : 7,
					slidesToScroll : 1,
					slide : ".slide",
					draggable : false,
					infinite: true,
					responsive: [
					    {
						    breakpoint: 1024,
						    settings: {
						    	slidesToShow: 4,
						        slidesToScroll: 1
						    }
					    },
					    {
						    breakpoint: 640,
						    settings: {
						    	slidesToShow: 2,
						        slidesToScroll: 1
						    }
					    }
					]
				});

				cb(null);
			},
			magnific : function(cb) {
				root.find('[data-sv-play]').magnificPopup({
				  type:'inline',
				  midClick: true // Allow opening popup on middle mouse click. Always set it to true if you don't provide alternative source in href.
				});

				cb(null);
			}
		}, function(err) {
			if (err) { throw err; }
		});


	});
           </script>
          </div>
         </div>

                <div class="slick-controls" id="passion_slick_controls">
                 <div class="slick-nav slick_nav">
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <script>
            require(['jquery', 'sv_siteSlick'], function($) {
		var root = $('[data-guid="6739d88b-4085-45d1-a838-f514bd43bdcc"]');
		var imgsToLoad = window.innerWidth > 1025 ? 5 : window.innerWidth > 768 ? 4 : 1;

		init_passion_slick();

		if (window.innerWidth > 640) {
			root.find('.item[data-index="2"]').addClass('open');

			for (var i = 0; i < imgsToLoad; i++) {
				setSrc(root.find('.item[data-index="' + (i + 1) + '"] img'));
			}
		} else {
			setSrc(root.find('.item img'));
		}

		function setSrc(node, checkEdges) {
			var _checkEdges = checkEdges || false;
			var i = 0;
			var limit = node.length;

			node.each(function() {
				if (_checkEdges && i === 0) { setSrc($(this).closest('.item').prev().find('img')); }

				i++;

				if (!$(this).hasClass('loaded')) {
					$(this).attr('src', $(this).attr('data-src'));
					$(this).addClass('loaded');
				}

				if (_checkEdges && i === limit) { setSrc($(this).closest('.item').next().find('img')); }
			});
		}

		/*----------  Init Passion Slick  ----------*/

		function init_passion_slick() {
			var $slick = root.find('[data-sv-passion]');

			if ($slick.length) {
				var $slick_controls = root.find('#passion_slick_controls');
				var $slick_nav = $slick_controls.find('.slick_nav');

				$slick.on('init', function(event, slick) {
					var slideCount = slick.slideCount;
					setSrc(root.find(".item[data-index=" + slideCount + "] img"), true);
					handle_slides();
				}).on("beforeChange", function(event, slick, current, next) {
					var slideCount = slick.slideCount;
					if (current - next > 0 ){
						setSrc(root.find(".item[data-index=" + (next + 1) + "] img"), true);
					} else {
						setSrc(root.find(".item[data-slick-index=" + (next + 4) + "] img"), true);
					}
				});

				$slick.slick({
					speed: 300,
					dots: false,
					arrows: true,
					infinite: true,
					slidesToShow: 4,
					draggable: false,
					slidesToScroll: 1,
					autoplaySpeed: 2000,
					adaptiveHeight: false,
					variableWidth: true,
					appendArrows: $slick_nav,
					lazyLoad: 'ondemand',
					prevArrow: '<span class="slick-arrow slick-prev slick_prev"><span class="fa fa-angle-left"></span></span>',
					nextArrow: '<span class="slick-arrow slick-next slick_next"><span class="fa fa-angle-right"></span></span>',
					responsive:[
						{
							breakpoint: 1025,
							settings: {
								slidesToShow: 3,
							}
						},
						{
							breakpoint: 768,
							settings: {
								slidesToShow: 2,
								variableWidth: true,
							}
						},
						{
							breakpoint: 640,
							settings: {
								slidesToShow: 1,
								variableWidth : false,
							}
						}
					]
				});

				function handle_slides() {
					var $item = $slick.find('.item');

					$item.off('click').on('click', function() {
						if (!$(this).hasClass('open')) {
							$item.removeClass('open');
							$(this).addClass('open');
						}
					});
				}
			}
		}
	});
           </script>

            <script>
             require(["jquery", 'plugins_common_custom_searchbox'], function($, searchbox) {
		function showMulti(num){
			var next= num+1;
			$('.rem_flight'+num).hide();
			$('.add_flight'+num).hide();
			$('.air_flight_'+next).slideDown();
		}
		function hideMulti(num){
			var prev= num-1;
			$('.air_flight_'+num).slideUp();
			$('.rem_flight'+prev).show();
			$('.add_flight'+prev).show();
		}
		$(document).ready(function() {
			$('#rs_search_multi').searchbox({
				refid:4098,
				environment: "prod",
				hotel:{
					elements:{
						form:".rs_hotel_form",
						chk_in:".rs_chk_in, .rs_chk_in_calendar, .rs_date_chk_in",
						chk_out:".rs_chk_out, .rs_chk_out_calendar, .rs_date_chk_out",
						chk_in_display:".rs_date_chk_in",
						chk_out_display:".rs_date_chk_out"
					},
					calendar:{
						output_format:"<div class='rs_mobi_chk_day'>[d]</div><div class='rs_mobi_chk_month'>[F]</div>"
					},
					select_name:true
				},
				car:{
					elements:{
						form:".rs_car_form",
						chk_in:".rs_chk_in, .rs_chk_in_calendar, .rs_date_chk_in",
						chk_out:".rs_chk_out, .rs_chk_out_calendar, .rs_date_chk_out",
						chk_in_display:".rs_date_chk_in",
						chk_out_display:".rs_date_chk_out",
					},
					calendar:{
						output_format:"<div class='rs_mobi_chk_day'>[d]</div><div class='rs_mobi_chk_month'>[F]</div>",
					}
				},
				air: {
					elements: {
						form: ".rs_air_form",
						chk_in:".rs_chk_in, .rs_chk_in_calendar, .rs_date_chk_in",
						chk_out:".rs_chk_out, .rs_chk_out_calendar, .rs_date_chk_out",
						chk_in_display: '.rs_mobiin',
						chk_in1_display: '.rs_mobi1',
						chk_out_display: '.rs_mobiout',
					},
					calendar: {
						output_format: '<div class="rs_mobi_chk_day">[d]</div><div class="rs_mobi_chk_month">[F]</div>'
					},
					select_name:true
				},
				vp:{
					elements: {
						form:".rs_vp_form",
						chk_in:".rs_chk_in, .rs_chk_in_calendar, .rs_date_chk_in",
						chk_out:".rs_chk_out, .rs_chk_out_calendar, .rs_date_chk_out",
						chk_in_display:".rs_date_chk_in",
						chk_out_display:".rs_date_chk_out",
					},
					calendar: {
						output_format: '<div class="rs_mobi_chk_day">[d]</div><div class="rs_mobi_chk_month">[F]</div>',
					},
					select_name:true
				}
			});
			if( /Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry|IEMobile|Opera Mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent) ) {
				$("<link/>", {
				   rel: "stylesheet",
				   type: "text/css",
				   href: "css/mobile_search.css"
				}).appendTo("head");
			}
			$('.same-location').click(function(){
				 $(".rs_droppff_div").hide();
				 $('.rs_pickup_div').removeClass('rs_half_width');
				 $('#different_return').attr('checked', false);
			});
			$('.diff-location').click(function(){
				 $(".rs_droppff_div").show();
				 $('.rs_pickup_div').addClass('rs_half_width');
				 $('#different_return').attr('checked', true);
			});
			$('.round-trip').click(function(){
				$('#air_round_trip').show();
				$('#air_one_way').hide();
				$('#air_multi_dest').hide();
			});
			$('.one-way').click(function(){
				$('#air_round_trip').hide();
				$('#air_one_way').show();
				$('#air_multi_dest').hide();
			});
			$('.multi-city').click(function(){
				$('#air_round_trip').hide();
				$('#air_one_way').hide();
				$('#air_multi_dest').show();
			});
			var $icons = $('.rs_tabs');
		    	$icons.click(function(){
		       $icons.removeClass('highlight_tab');
		       $(this).addClass('highlight_tab');
		    });
			var $air_options = $('.rs_air_option');
		    	$air_options.click(function(){
		       $air_options.removeClass('air_highlight');
		       $(this).addClass('air_highlight');
		    });
		    var $car_options = $('.rs_car_option');
		    	$car_options.click(function(){
		       $car_options.removeClass('car_highlight');
		       $(this).addClass('car_highlight');
		    });
			$(".rs_tabs").on("click", function(){
				var futureTab = $(this).data("tab"),
					$selectedForm = $("."+futureTab);
				if ($selectedForm.hasClass("rs_searchbox_hide")) {
					$selectedForm.removeClass('rs_searchbox_hide').siblings(".rs_search_form").addClass("rs_searchbox_hide");
				}
			});
			$('.rs_product_select').on('change',function(){
	   			var $option = $('.rs_product_select').val();
	   			$('.rs_search_form').addClass('rs_searchbox_hide');
	   			$('.rs_'+$option+'_form').removeClass('rs_searchbox_hide');
	   			$('.rs_tabs').removeClass('highlight_tab');
	   			$('#rs_'+$option+'_tab').addClass('highlight_tab');
			});
		});
	});
            </script>
           </div>
          </div>
         </section>

           <script>
            require(['jquery', 'lodash'], function($, lodash) {
		var root = $('[data-guid="ee543ce4-0b60-4a92-87ef-8d3a7b848458"]');
		var flippedSlidesLg = ['lesiure-a', 'leisure-c', 'leisure-hs', 'leisure-m', 'leisure-fv'];
		var flippsedSlideMd = ['leisure-z', 'leisure-w', 'lesiure-w', 'leisure-k', 'lesiure-r', 'leisure-er', 'leisure-wf'];

		root.on('click', '[data-map-pane-inner]', function(e) {
			e.stopPropagation();
		});

		root.on('click', '[data-map-shade]', function() {
			root.find('[data-map-pane]').removeClass('active');
			root.removeClass('map-scroll-open');
		});

		root.on('click', '[data-map-pane]', function() {
			$(this).removeClass('active');
			root.removeClass('map-scroll-open');
		});

		root.on('click', '[data-map-trigger]', function() {
			if (window.innerWidth > 640) { return; }

			root.find('[data-map-pane]').addClass('active');
			root.addClass('map-scroll-open');
		});

		root.on('click', '[data-close]', function() {
			$(this).closest('[data-slide]').removeClass('active');
		});

		root.on('click', '[data-id]', function() {
			var id = $(this).attr('data-id');
			var dimensions = $(this).offset();
			var moreDimensions = $(this)[0].getBoundingClientRect();

			root.find('[data-slide].active').each(function() {
				$(this).removeClass('active');
			});

			var slide = root.find('[data-slide="' + id + '"]');
			var top = (dimensions.top + (moreDimensions.height / 2)) - root.offset().top;

			var left;
			if (window.innerWidth > 1024) {
				left = flippedSlidesLg.indexOf(id) > 0 ? (dimensions.left + moreDimensions.width) : dimensions.left;
			} else {
				left = flippsedSlideMd.indexOf(id) > 0 ? dimensions.left : (dimensions.left + moreDimensions.width);
			}

			slide.css({
				"top" : top,
				"left" : left
			});
			slide.addClass('active');
		});

		var listenResize = function() {
			root.find('[data-slide]').each(function() {
				$(this).removeClass('active');
			});
		}
		$(window).on('resize', lodash.debounce(listenResize, 500));
	});
           </script>

                  {{~exec(function() {
	helpers.var.source = data.widgetArgs.data.source === 'feed' ? data.widgetArgs.data.selectFeed : 'slides';

	// Generate a formatted date based on startDate/endDate and whether the we're using the offer's feed
  	var formattedDate = function(fmt, offersPrefix) {
		var fmt = fmt || 'LL';

		if (helpers.var.source === 'plugins_offers_offers') {
			var offersPrefix = offersPrefix || 'Valid: ';
			if (this.startDate && this.endDate) {
				return offersPrefix + this.startDate.format(fmt) + ' - ' + this.endDate.format(fmt);
			} if (!this.startDate && this.endDate) {
				return offersPrefix + 'Ending ' + this.startDate.format(fmt);
			} else if (!this.endDate && this.startDate) {
				return offersPrefix + 'Starting ' + this.endDate.format(fmt);
			}
			return 'Valid: Always';
		} else if (this.startDate) {
			if(this.endDate !== undefined && this.startDate.isSame(this.endDate, 'month')) {
				return this.startDate.format('MMMM D') + ' - ' + this.endDate.format('D') + ", " + this.startDate.format('YYYY');
			} else {
				return this.startDate.format(fmt) + (this.endDate ? ' - ' + this.endDate.format(fmt) : '');
			}
		}
	};

	// Generate a cleaned desciption that trim text and strips HTML.
  	var plainDescription = function(limit, options) {
		var options = options || { ellipsis: true };
		var nohtml = helpers.plugins.stringLib.stripHtml(this.description);
		return limit ? helpers.plugins.stringLib.substringOnWord(nohtml, limit, options) : nohtml;
	};

	// Cleanup feed data
  	data.items.forEach(function(item) {
		// Fix event date to unify startDate/endDate
		if (helpers.var.source === 'plugins_events_events') {
			if (data.widgetArgs.data.data_groupBy === 'date') {
				item.startDate = item.nextDate = helpers.plugins.clientMoment(item.date);
			} else {
				item.startDate = item.nextDate;
			}
			if (item.endDate && item.startDate.isSame(item.endDate, 'day')) {
				delete item.endDate;
			}
		}

    	// Add a helper boolean to let us know if we have dates
		var dateCollections = ['plugins_events_events', 'plugins_offers_offers'];
		item.hasDates = dateCollections.indexOf(helpers.var.source) > -1 || (item.startDate || item.endDate);

		// If there is no asset or there is an invalid asset, create a new one using the placeholder
    	if (item.asset && item.asset.resource && !item.asset.resource.getUrl) {
      		item.asset.resource = helpers.plugins.cloudinary.createResource(item.asset.resource);
    	}

	    if (item.asset && item.asset.type === 'video') {
	    	item.asset.videoresource = new helpers.plugins.videoLib.Resource({
	        	id : item.asset.videoid,
	        	type : item.asset.videotype
	    	});
	    }

	    // If there is no asset or there is an invalid asset, create a new one using the placeholder
	    if (!item.asset || !item.asset.resource) {
			item.asset = {
				resource : helpers.plugins.cloudinary.createResource({
		        	imageUrl : helpers.plugins.sv_site.siteConfig.custom.placeholderImageUrl
		      	}),
				alt_text : item.title,
				type : 'image',
				isPlaceholder : true
			};
	    }

	    // Create an onerror asset using the placeholder
	    item.onErrorAsset = {
	    	resource : helpers.plugins.cloudinary.createResource({
	        	imageUrl : helpers.plugins.sv_site.siteConfig.custom.placeholderImageUrl
	    	}),
	    	type : 'image'
	    };

	    // Ensure there is always alt_text
	    item.asset.alt_text = item.asset.alt_text ? item.asset.alt_text : item.title;

	    // Add date and description format helper to item
		item.formattedDate = formattedDate;
		item.plainDescription = plainDescription;

	    // Set the feed type at the item level
	    if (helpers.var.source === 'plugins_events_events') {
	    	item.feedType = "event";
	    } else if (helpers.var.source === 'plugins_offers_offers') {
	    	item.feedType = "offer";
	    } else if (helpers.var.source === 'plugins_listings_listings') {
	    	item.feedType = "listing";
	    } else if (helpers.var.source === 'plugins_blog_leisure_blog_posts') {
	    	item.feedType = "Blog";
	    }


	    //item has date
	    if (item.startDate) {
	    	item.hasDate = true
	    }


	});
})}}

                  {{~exec(function() {
	helpers.var.source = data.widgetArgs.data.source === 'feed' ? data.widgetArgs.data.selectFeed : 'slides';

	// Generate a formatted date based on startDate/endDate and whether the we're using the offer's feed
  	var formattedDate = function(fmt, offersPrefix) {
		var fmt = fmt || 'LL';

		if (helpers.var.source === 'plugins_offers_offers') {
			var offersPrefix = offersPrefix || 'Valid: ';
			if (this.startDate && this.endDate) {
				return offersPrefix + this.startDate.format(fmt) + ' - ' + this.endDate.format(fmt);
			} if (!this.startDate && this.endDate) {
				return offersPrefix + 'Ending ' + this.startDate.format(fmt);
			} else if (!this.endDate && this.startDate) {
				return offersPrefix + 'Starting ' + this.endDate.format(fmt);
			}
			return 'Valid: Always';
		} else if (this.startDate) {
			if(this.endDate !== undefined && this.startDate.isSame(this.endDate, 'month')) {
				return this.startDate.format('MMMM D') + ' - ' + this.endDate.format('D') + ", " + this.startDate.format('YYYY');
			} else {
				return this.startDate.format(fmt) + (this.endDate ? ' - ' + this.endDate.format(fmt) : '');
			}
		}
	};

	// Generate a cleaned desciption that trim text and strips HTML.
  	var plainDescription = function(limit, options) {
		var options = options || { ellipsis: true };
		var nohtml = helpers.plugins.stringLib.stripHtml(this.description);
		return limit ? helpers.plugins.stringLib.substringOnWord(nohtml, limit, options) : nohtml;
	};

	// Cleanup feed data
  	data.items.forEach(function(item) {
		// Fix event date to unify startDate/endDate
		if (helpers.var.source === 'plugins_events_events') {
			if (data.widgetArgs.data.data_groupBy === 'date') {
				item.startDate = item.nextDate = helpers.plugins.clientMoment(item.date);
			} else {
				item.startDate = item.nextDate;
			}
			if (item.endDate && item.startDate.isSame(item.endDate, 'day')) {
				delete item.endDate;
			}
		}

    	// Add a helper boolean to let us know if we have dates
		var dateCollections = ['plugins_events_events', 'plugins_offers_offers'];
		item.hasDates = dateCollections.indexOf(helpers.var.source) > -1 || (item.startDate || item.endDate);

		// If there is no asset or there is an invalid asset, create a new one using the placeholder
    	if (item.asset && item.asset.resource && !item.asset.resource.getUrl) {
      		item.asset.resource = helpers.plugins.cloudinary.createResource(item.asset.resource);
    	}

	    if (item.asset && item.asset.type === 'video') {
	    	item.asset.videoresource = new helpers.plugins.videoLib.Resource({
	        	id : item.asset.videoid,
	        	type : item.asset.videotype
	    	});
	    }

	    // If there is no asset or there is an invalid asset, create a new one using the placeholder
	    if (!item.asset || !item.asset.resource) {
			item.asset = {
				resource : helpers.plugins.cloudinary.createResource({
		        	imageUrl : helpers.plugins.sv_site.siteConfig.custom.placeholderImageUrl
		      	}),
				alt_text : item.title,
				type : 'image',
				isPlaceholder : true
			};
	    }

	    // Create an onerror asset using the placeholder
	    item.onErrorAsset = {
	    	resource : helpers.plugins.cloudinary.createResource({
	        	imageUrl : helpers.plugins.sv_site.siteConfig.custom.placeholderImageUrl
	    	}),
	    	type : 'image'
	    };

	    // Ensure there is always alt_text
	    item.asset.alt_text = item.asset.alt_text ? item.asset.alt_text : item.title;

	    // Add date and description format helper to item
		item.formattedDate = formattedDate;
		item.plainDescription = plainDescription;

	    // Set the feed type at the item level
	    if (helpers.var.source === 'plugins_events_events') {
	    	item.feedType = "event";
	    } else if (helpers.var.source === 'plugins_offers_offers') {
	    	item.feedType = "offer";
	    } else if (helpers.var.source === 'plugins_listings_listings') {
	    	item.feedType = "listing";
	    } else if (helpers.var.source === 'plugins_blog_leisure_blog_posts') {
	    	item.feedType = "Blog";
	    }


	    //item has date
	    if (item.startDate) {
	    	item.hasDate = true
	    }


	});
})}}

                   <script>
                    require(['jquery', 'plugins_addthis'], function($) {
		var root = $('[data-guid="03dd3b25-0d87-4b10-900a-76748434b753"]');
		var standard = root.find('[data-sv-addthis-standard]');
		var footerTop = root.find('[data-sv-addthis-top]');
		var footerBottom = root.find('[data-sv-addthis-bottom]');

		root.find('a').on('click', function(e) {
			e.preventDefault();
		});

		if (root.closest('footer').length > 0) {
			$('[data-sv-addthis-top-container]').replaceWith(footerTop);
			footerTop.removeClass('hide');

			$('[data-sv-addthis-bottom-container]').replaceWith(footerBottom);
			footerBottom.removeClass('hide');
		} else {
			standard.removeClass('hide');
		}
	});
                   </script>

		var readCookie = function(name) {
			var nameEQ = name + "=";
			var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
			for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
				var c = ca[i];
				while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
				if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
			}
			return null;
		}

		/* In some cases the subdomain cookie won't get deleted so google translate will retain the last
		   translation when you navigate to a new page. This function will delete the sub-domain cookie as well. */
		var deleteCookie = function(name) {
			var delCookie = name + '=;expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT; path=/';
			document.cookie = delCookie;
			document.cookie = delCookie + '; domain=.'+window.location.host;
			document.cookie = delCookie + '; domain=.'+window.location.hostname.split('.').slice(-2).join('.');
		}

		/* Preselects the current option. In some cases the hash can disappear so we can also check for
		   the google translate cookie if there is no hash language code */
		var gthash = window.location.hash.match(/\#googtrans\([A-Za-z_0-9\-]+\|([A-Za-z_0-9\-]+)\)/);
		var gtcookie = String(readCookie('googtrans')).match(/\/[A-Za-z_0-9\-]+\/([A-Za-z_0-9\-]+)/);
		var lang =  gthash !== null ? gthash[1] : gtcookie !== null ? gtcookie[1] : "";
		$(".googleTranslateDropdown").val(lang);

		var gtTranslate = function(lang) {
			if (lang === "") return;
			if (lang === 'en') deleteCookie('googtrans');
			window.location.hash = lang === 'en' ? '' : "#googtrans(en|" + lang + ")";
			window.location.reload(true);
		}

		$('body').addClass(lang);

		root.find(".googleTranslateDropdown").change(function() {
			gtTranslate($(this).val());

		});
		var googleContent = $('[data-sv-googletranslate]').clone(true);

		$('[data-mobile-googletranslate]').append(googleContent);

	});
                </script>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
          </section>
         </footer>
         <script>
          // Should be in footer. We show all the previously hidden parents of the calendar
	require(["jquery", "domReady!"], function($) {
		if (location.search.indexOf('action=popupCal') > -1 && document.body.querySelectorAll('.lookup-calHolder')) {
			$('.lookup-calHolder').parents().show().addClass('crm-calendar-parent');
		}
	});
         </script>

   <script>
    require(["jquery", "sv_stringLib", "sv_clientLib", "lodash"], function($, stringLib, clientLib, lodash) {
			var root = $('[data-guid="73a46a7d-221f-4b2b-abb8-38f1de6e5eac"]');

			var mobileAd = root.find("[data-sv-mobiledtn-mobilead]");
			var content = mobileAd.find(".content");
			var closeButton = mobileAd.find("[data-sv-mobiledtn-close]");
			var storageKey = "mobile_dtn_ad_hide";
			var sessionAvailable = clientLib.sessionStorageAvailable();

			// show ad if session not available or if it doesn't contain our hide session var
			var showAd = sessionAvailable === false || window.sessionStorage.getItem(storageKey) !== "true";

			closeButton.on("click", function(e) {
				e.preventDefault();

				// if we have session storage, prevent it from appearing on future page views this session
				if (sessionAvailable) { window.sessionStorage.setItem(storageKey, "true"); }

				showAd = false;
				mobileAd.remove();
				render();
			});

			var render = function() {
				// according to DTN the philosophy should be show this banner if the site in general is in mobile or tablet view regardless of device (determined by width only)
				var isMobile = window.innerWidth < 1024;

				var displayAd = isMobile === true && showAd === true;
				root.toggleClass("hasMobileAd", displayAd);

				if (displayAd && content.children().length === 0) {
					// executes the dtn code if the ad should be displayed and the ad wasn't already rendered
					var html = stringLib.decodeScriptTags(root.find("[data-sv-mobiledtn-adcode]").html());
					content.html(html);
					root.find("#dtnContainer").append(closeButton);
				}
			};

			render();

			// allows cms preview device switcher to work, without having to hit preview refresh button
			$(window).on("resize", lodash.debounce(render, 300));
		});
   </script>
